FNV SUN PROJECTION DEEP CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Can Psycho derive sun direction from Sky -> Sun -> RootNode without invasive hooks?
2. Which camera basis/frustum fields are valid at scene/final image-space phases?
3. Can CPU code project sun direction to screen UV using proven fields only?
4. Which read path should fail closed for compatibility with NVR/TESReloaded/Shader Loader?

======================================================================
LAYOUT CONTRACT TO PROVE
======================================================================
Sun source:
  Sky singleton: *(Sky**)0x011DEA20
  Sky::sun: Sky + 0x28
  Sun inherits SkyObject: RootNode at Sun + 0x04
  Sun direction candidate: normalize(SunRoot->m_localTransform.pos)
  Candidate local transform pos: RootNode + 0x58
Camera source:
  BSShaderManager::pCurrentCamera: *(NiCamera**)0x011F917C
  Current proven near/far: camera + 0xEC/+0xF0
  Prior output says camera +0x94 is not a matrix; do not use it as WorldToCam.
  Need proof for basis fields copied by 0x00B5E870 and frustum/global projection fields.
Target CPU constants:
  sun UV, sun available, forward-facing amount, sun color/glare, and optional view-space direction.
